 sansadeey samiti kii siforeeshon ko darkinar karte hue centre sarkaar ne buudhvaar ko jaghanya aparaadhon ke aaropee 16 se 18 saal ke kishoravay aparaadhiyon par vayaskon ke liye bane kanoonon ke tahat mukadmaa chalaane ke prastaav ko manjuuri pradaan kar di
 Communications Minister Ravi Shankar Prasad told reporters after the cabinet meeting, 'the cabinet has approved amendments to the Juvenile Justice (care and Protection of Children) Act where juvenile offenders aged 16 to 18 years are charged under the Indian Penal Code
 They can be prosecuted if they are accused of heinous crimes
 ‚Äô The subject was brought to the Cabinet about a fortnight ago but it was dropped from the agenda at the last minute and it was decided that an informal group of ministers would investigate the issue
 sansadeey sthaayee samiti kii siforeeshon ko naamanzoor karte hue mahila evam bal vikaas mantralay ne is prastaav par aage badhane kaa faisla kiya
 The Supreme Court also recently said that the provisions of the Juvenile Justice Act need to be reviewed in cases involving juveniles committing crimes such as rape, murder, robbery and acid attacks
 cabinet baithak main kai mantriyon ne prastaav kaa yah kehete hue samarthan kiya ki balaatkaar jaise aparaadh ke aaropee vyakti ko vayask kii tarah liya janaa chahie
 a senior minister gave this information after the meeting
 ‚Äònayaa prastaavit adhinium (sanshodhan vidheyak) vyavastha karata he ki aise maamle main jahaan jaghanya aparaadh ko 16 se 18 aayu varg ke vyakti ne anjaam diya he to uskaa adhyayan kishor nyaay board karegaa or yah pataa lagayegaa ki kya aparaadh ek ‚Äòbalak‚Äô ke taur par kiya gaya he yaa ‚Äòvayask‚Äô ke taur par
 According to a government statement, 'since this assessment will be done by a board consisting of psychiatrists and social experts, this will ensure that the juvenile's rights are properly protected if the offender has committed the crime as a child
 aise main maamle kii sunwaayee akalan ke aadhaar par ek kishor apradhi yaa ek vayask ke taur par hogi
 ' sanshodhit vidheyak main anathon, besahaara or samarpan karne vaale bacchon ko god lene kii prakriya ko bhi durust karne kaa prastaav he
 In this, statutory status has been fixed for Child Adoption Resource Tribunal (CARA)
 tippaniyan The bill also proposes social integration measures and several rehabilitation measures for institutional and non-institutionalized children
 isamen puri tarah nae upaay ke taur par pryojit or dekhbhaal kii bhi vyavastha kii gayi he
 Compulsory registration is also proposed for all institutions that provide child care
 prastaavit vidheyak main gaiyrkanoonee god lene, bal dekhbhaal sansthaanon main kadi sajaa, aatankwaadi samoohon dwaara bacchon kaa istemaal or viklang bacchon ke khilaaf aparaadhon jaise nae aparaadhon ko bhi shaamil kiya gaya he
 The most important amendment is the removal of clause seven, which relates to hearing an adult as an adult only when he is over 21 years of age for committing heinous crime
 sanshodhit vidheyak ko chaalu bajet satr ke dauraan sansad main laayaa jayega
 Official sources gave this information
 sanchaar mantri ravishankar prasad ne cabinet baithak ke baad samvaadadaataaon ko bataaya, ‚Äòcabinet ne kishor nyaay (bacchon kii dekhbhaal or sangrakshan) adhinium main sanshodhano ko manjuuri pradaan kar di he jahaan 16 se 18 saal aayu varg ke kishor aparaadhiyon par bhartiya dand samhita ke tahat mukadmaa chalaaya ja saktaa he, yadi ve jaghanya aparaadhon ke aaropee hai
 ' yah vishay kareeb ek pakhwaade pehle cabinet ke samaksh laayaa gaya tha lekin antim kshanon main ise agenda se hataa diya gaya tha or yah tay kiya gaya tha ki mantriyon kaa ek anaupchaarik samooh is mudde kii padtaal karegaa
 Rejecting the recommendations of the Parliamentary Standing Committee, the Ministry of Women and Child Development decided to move forward on this proposal
 supreme court ne bhi haal hi main kaha tha ki balaatkaar, hatya, dakaiti or tejaab hamalon jaise aparaadhon ko kishoron dwaara anjaam die jane ke maamalon main kishor nyaay adhinium ke praavdhaanon kii samiksha kii jarurat he
 In the cabinet meeting, several ministers supported the proposal, saying that a person accused of a crime like rape should be treated as an adult
 ek varisht mantri ne baithak ke baad yah jaankaree di
 The new proposed Act (amendment Bill) provides that in a case where heinous crime has been committed by a person between the age group of 16 to 18, the Juvenile Justice Board will study it and find out if the crime is committed as a 'child'
 Has been done or as an 'adult'
 ek sarkari bayaan ke anusaar, ‚Äòchunki yah akalan ek aise board dwaara kiya jayega jisamen manochikitsak or samaaj visheshgy honge, to isse yah sunishchit ho sakegaa ki agar apradhi ne bataur balak aparaadh ko anjaam diya he to kishor ke adhikaron kaa uchit sangrakshan ho
 In this case, the case will be heard on the basis of assessment as a juvenile delinquent or an adult
 ‚Äô The amended bill also proposes to reform the adoption process of orphans, destitutes and surrendering children
 isamen bal dattak sansaadhan adhikaran (sieaare) ke liye sanvidhik darja tay kiya gaya he
 The comments vidheyak main sansthagat or gaiyr sansthagat bacchon ke liye saamaajik ekikaran upaay or kai punarvaas upayon kaa bhi prastaav kiya gaya he
 It has also sponsored and taken care of as a completely new measure
 bacchon kii dekhbhaal kii suvidha muhaiyaa karaane vaale sabhi sansthaanon ke liye anivaary panjikaran kaa bhi prastaav he
 The proposed bill also includes new crimes such as illegal adoption, stricter punishment in child care institutions, use of children by terrorist groups and crimes against children with disabilities
 sabase mahatvapurn sanshodhan upbandh saat ko hataanaa he jo kisi vyakti dwaara jaghanya aparaadh kiye jane ke liye 21 saal se adhik umr hone par hi uske khilaaf vayask kii tarah sunwaayee kiye jane se sambandhit he

 com / uxszxvmhol gyanpith puraskaar se sammanit naatakkaar or abhinayta girish karnad ne kaha ki 18veen sadi ke mysore ke shaasha tipu sultan agar muslim nahin hindu hote to unhen maratha shaasha chhatrapati shivaji ke samaan darja miltaa
 Karnad said in another disputed statement that it would have been 'appropriate' if the Bangalore International Airport at Devanhalli was named after Tipu Sultan instead of Kempegowda
 kempegauda vijaynagar samrajya ke tahat jagirdaar the, jinhone 1537 main bengaluru kii sthapana kii thi
 Karnad said, 'I feel that if Tipu Sultan were not a Hindu, he would have got the same status in Karnataka as Shivaji Maharaj enjoys in Maharashtra
 ' unhone kaha ki tipu ko unki dharmik aasthaa ke kaaran yah sammaan nahin mila
 'because it is happening today that our scholars and leaders see someone's religion and caste first
 
 
 ' unhone kaha, 'is prakaar ke moolyankan ke kaaran tipu sultan ke saath anyaay hua he
 
 
 ' mashhoor kannada naatakkaar or abhinayta kii yah tippanee aise samay ai he, jab rajya sarkaar ne tipu sultan kii jayanti par samarohon kaa aayojan kiya he
 In the presence of Chief Minister Siddaramaiah, the program was organized in the state secretariat amid tight security
 bijepi rajyavyapee samarohon kaa bahishkaar kar rahi he
 Many organizations have also opposed this, according to whom Tipu Sultan was 'religiously staunch and anti-kannada'
 pradarshnon ke bich kodagu jile ke madikeri main huyi hinsa main ek vyakti kii maut ho gai
 Targeting those who called Tipu Sultan 'anti-kannada and anti-hindu', Karnad said, "today, we are celebrating this day as Deepawali and Tipu Sultan Day, we can also celebrate it as Bihar Day
 ' bihar diwas sambandhi unki tippanee saaf taur se bijepi par nishaanaa tha, jise bihar vidhansabha chunaav main baari haar kaa saamana karnaa padaa he
 Karnad has been opposing the BJP ideologically
 tippaniyan Siddaramaiah, expressing the same view as Karnad's opinion, said, '
 
 
 agar vah hindu ke rup main paidaa hote to karnataka or puure desh main unhen vahi sammaan miltaa jo shivaji ko miltaa he
 'he said,' We should not look at a person from the point of view of his religion or caste, but keeping in mind the good work done by him for the people
 ' Along with this, Karnad said it would have been nice that the Bangalore International Airport at Devanhalli would be named after Tipu Sultan instead of Kempegowda, as Kempegowda was not a freedom fighter
 unhone kaha ki hawaii adda kaa naam tipu sultan ke naam par rakhana adhik uchit hoga, kyonki devanhalli unka janmasthan tha
 Karnad said, 'I am aware that what i am saying will be debated
 
 
 jaisaa ki ham jaanate hai ki kolkata hawaii adde kaa naam netaji subhaashachandr bose ke naam par he, mumbai hawaondde kaa naam shivaji maharaj ke naam par he, lekin karnataka main hamane iskaa naam kempegauda ke naam par rakhaa he
 Taking a dig at Karnad's remarks about the name of the airport, the BJP said that they have insulted the founder of Bengaluru on an issue which is a 'closed chapter'
 karnad ne ek anya vivaadit bayaan main kaha ki 'uchit' hota agar devanhalli main bengaluru antarrashtriya hawaii adde kaa naam kempegauda ke badale tipu sultan ke naam par hota
 Kempegowda was a vassal under the Vijayanagara Empire, who founded Bengaluru in 1537
 karnad ne kaha, 'main mahasoos karata hum ki agar tipu sultan muslim nahin hindu hote to unhen karnataka main vahi darja miltaa jo maharashtra main shivaji maharaj ko praapt he
 He said that Tipu did not get this honor due to his religious faith
 'kyonki aaj yah ho rahaa he ki hamaare vidwaan or netaa kisi kaa dharm or jati pehle dekhte hai
 
 
 He said, 'an injustice has been done to Tipu Sultan because of this type of evaluation
 
 
 ' This remark by the famous Kannada playwright and actor has come at a time when the state government has organized celebrations on the birth anniversary of Tipu Sultan
 mukhyamantri siddharamaiya kii maujuudagi main yahaan rajya sachivalay main kadi suraksha vyavastha ke bich kaarykram kaa aayojan kiya gaya
 The BJP is boycotting statewide celebrations
 kai sanghathanon ne bhi iskaa virodh kiya he, jinaki najar main tipu sultan 'dharmik rup se kattar or kannada virdohi' the
 One person was killed in violence in Madikeri in Kodagu district amid protests
 tipu sultan ko 'kannada virdohi or hindu virdohi' kehane waalon par nishaanaa sadhate hue karnad ne kaha, 'aaj, ham yah din deepawali or tipu sultan diwas ke rup main manaa rahe hai, ham ise bihar diwas ke taur par bhi manaa sakate hai
 His comment on 'bihar Day' was clearly aimed at the BJP, which has suffered heavy losses in the Bihar Assembly elections
 karnad bijepi kaa vaicharik virodh karte rahe hai
 The comments karnad kii raay ke samaan hi vichaar vyakt karte hue siddharamaiya ne kaha, '
 
 
 If he were born as a Hindu, he would have got the same respect that Shivaji gets in Karnataka and the whole country
 ' unhone kaha, 'hamen kisi vyakti ko uske dharm yaa jati ke najariye se nahin, balki logon ke liye unke dwaara karaae gaye achche kaam ko dhyaan main rakhkar dekhnaa chahie
 ' iske saath hi karnad ne kaha ki acha hota ki devanhalli ke bengaluru antarrashtriya hawaii adde kaa naam kempegauda ke badale tipu sultan ke naam par rakhaa jaataa, kyonki kempegauda swatantraaa senaanee nahin the
 He said that it would be more appropriate to name the airport after Tipu Sultan, as Devanhalli was his birthplace
 karnad ne kaha, 'main is baat se avgat hum ki main jo kah rahaa hum, us par bahes hogi
 
 
 As we know that Kolkata airport is named after Netaji Subhash Chandra Bose, Mumbai airport is named after Shivaji Maharaj but in Karnataka we have named it after Kempegowda
 ' hawaii adde ke naam ko lekar karnad kii tippanee par bhaajapa ne nishaanaa sadhate hue kaha ki unhone begaluru ke sansthaapak kaa aise mudde par apmaan kiya he, jo 'band adhyay' he
 Karnad said, 'I feel that if Tipu Sultan were not a Hindu, he would have got the same status in Karnataka as Shivaji Maharaj enjoys in Maharashtra
 ' unhone kaha ki tipu ko unki dharmik aasthaa ke kaaran yah sammaan nahin mila
 'because it is happening today that our scholars and leaders see someone's religion and caste first
 
 
 ' unhone kaha, 'is prakaar ke moolyankan ke kaaran tipu sultan ke saath anyaay hua he
 
 
 ' mashhoor kannada naatakkaar or abhinayta kii yah tippanee aise samay ai he, jab rajya sarkaar ne tipu sultan kii jayanti par samarohon kaa aayojan kiya he
 In the presence of Chief Minister Siddaramaiah, the program was organized in the state secretariat amid tight security
 bijepi rajyavyapee samarohon kaa bahishkaar kar rahi he
 Many organizations have also opposed this, according to whom Tipu Sultan was 'religiously staunch and anti-kannada'
 pradarshnon ke bich kodagu jile ke madikeri main huyi hinsa main ek vyakti kii maut ho gai
 Targeting those who called Tipu Sultan 'anti-kannada and anti-hindu', Karnad said, "today, we are celebrating this day as Deepawali and Tipu Sultan Day, we can also celebrate it as Bihar Day
 ' bihar diwas sambandhi unki tippanee saaf taur se bijepi par nishaanaa tha, jise bihar vidhansabha chunaav main baari haar kaa saamana karnaa padaa he
 Karnad has been opposing the BJP ideologically
 tippaniyan Siddaramaiah, expressing the same view as Karnad's opinion, said, '
 
 
 agar vah hindu ke rup main paidaa hote to karnataka or puure desh main unhen vahi sammaan miltaa jo shivaji ko miltaa he
 'he said,' We should not look at a person from the point of view of his religion or caste, but keeping in mind the good work done by him for the people
 ' Along with this, Karnad said it would have been nice that the Bangalore International Airport at Devanhalli would be named after Tipu Sultan instead of Kempegowda, as Kempegowda was not a freedom fighter
 unhone kaha ki hawaii adda kaa naam tipu sultan ke naam par rakhana adhik uchit hoga, kyonki devanhalli unka janmasthan tha

 Tamil superstar Siddharth while talking to NDTV said that the floods in Tamil Nadu were historic and he was very angry for losing his house for the first time
 unhone kaha, ve un garib logon ke liye bhi dukhi the, jinhone ek din main apana bahut kuch kho diya
 Siddharth said, 'I was angry for losing my house for the first time
 teen studio, teen car or phir main un madhyavargeey logon ke liye bhi bura mahasoos kar rahaa tha jinhone ek hi din main apana bahut kuch kho diya
 He said, he was not in his house for the last 6 days
 unke ghar main pani bharaa hua tha
 Just now the water has completely come out and power has returned since yesterday evening
 soshal media dwaara utpann kii gai jabardast pratikriya ke kaaran ummid kii kiran sirf ye rahi ki pehali baar kisi prakritik aapadaa ke dauraan peediton se zyada bachaavkarmi vahaan maujuud the
 This trend is seen after the floods in Jammu and Kashmir last year
 somvaar ko kuddlor jile main baadh prabhavit 15 gaanvon kaa vyapak daura karne baad siddharth ne kaha, raahat pahunchane ke prayaason main ek taraf to soshal media vardaan he to duusari taraf yah abhishaap bhi he
 He said, often the old information is circulated repeatedly on social media and in this way the information transmitted many times becomes quite old
 unhone ek udhaaharan dete hue bataaya, 'aaj koi ek massej bhej saktaa he ki phalani jagah pani kii 5000 bottlen chahie
 This message will be broadcast on social media even after 6 days
 jabaki 6 din baad kisi ko un 5000 pani kii botalon kii jarurat nahin hogi or ve kooday ke dibbe main jaaengi
 ' kuddlor main raahat kaaryon par baat karte hue siddharth ne kaha, 'yahaan ke halaat bure the, lekin utane bhi bure nahin the jitna soshal media par prasaarit ho rahaa tha
 "at this time, there is no need for big containers of relief material like food, they will be caught on the highway by greedy people and will not even let them reach the needy
" is vakt logon ko bistar, kambal or aashray kii jarurat he
 Eventually people will need livelihood, so that they will be able to build their homes lost in this flood
 raahat kaaryon ko lekar tamilnadu sarkaar kii aalochana bhi ho rahi he
 When Siddharth was asked about this, he said, 'I personally do not see any deficiency in the way the administration is working
 'tippaniyan Siddharth said, 'I am neither in support of any government nor in opposition
 yah apni tarah kii ek anokhi aapadaa he
 i do not think that any state government will allow everything to end so easily in just 5 days
 ' unhone kaha, 'bharat araajaktaa ke siddhant par kaam karata he, yah maanav kii ichha se chalata he, jaruri nahin ki ise prashasan chalaae

 Due to the tremendous response generated by the social media, the only hope was that for the first time, during a natural disaster, more rescuers were present than the victims
 pichley saal jammu-kashmir main ai baadh ke baad ye pravriti dekhi ja rahi he
 After making extensive visits to 15 flood-affected villages in Cuddalore district on Monday, Siddharth said, "social media is a boon in efforts to provide relief and on the other side it is a curse
" unhone kaha, soshal media par aksar puraani jaankaree ko hi baar-baar prasaarit kiya jaataa he or is tarah se kai baar prasaarit jaankaree kaaphi puraani pad jaati he
 Giving an example, he said, 'today one can send a message that 5000 bottles of water are needed at such a place
 yah massej 6 din baad bhi soshal media par prasaarit ho rahaa hoga
 Whereas after 6 days no one will need those 5000 water bottles and they will go to the litter box
 ' Talking about relief operations in Cuddalore, Siddharth said, 'the conditions here were bad, but not as bad as was being circulated on social media
 ' unhone kaha, is samay khaanaa aadi raahat saamagree ke bade-bade container kii jarurat nahin he, unhen to haive par hi laalchee log hadap lenge or jaruratmand tak pahunchane bhi nahin denge
 Right now people need beds, blankets and shelter
 aakhirkaar logon ko aajeevika kii jarurat hogi, jisase ve is baadh main kho chuke apane ghar bana paaenge
 The Tamil Nadu government is also being criticized for the relief work
 jab siddharth se is bare main poocha gaya to unhone kaha, 'jis tarah se prashasan kaam kar rahaa he mujhe vyaktigat taur par isamen koi kami nahin dikh rahi he

 This is a unique disaster of its kind
 mujhe nahin lagata ki koi bhi rajya sarkaar sirf 5 din main sab kuch itani aasaani se khatm ho jane degi
 'he said,' India works on the principle of anarchy, it operates with the will of the human being, not necessarily by the administration

 is vakt repo rate ko 6 fisadi par hi rakhaa gaya tha
 What is Repo Rate? Repo rate is the rate at which banks take loans from RBI
 darasal jab bhi bainkon ke paas fund kii kami hoti he, to ve isaki bharpai karne ke liye kendriya bank se paise lete hai
 This loan given by RBI is available at a fixed rate
 yahi rate repo rate kehalaata he
 It is always decided by the Reserve Bank of India
 repo rate kyon badhaata he arabiai?bhartiya rigerv bank repo rate main katautee yaa badhotaree karne kaa faisla maujuuda or bhavishya main arthvyavastha ke sambhavit halaat ke aadhaar par letaa he
 The central bank increases the repo rate at most times when inflation in the country remains under pressure
 aise main ise niyantran main laane ke liye repo rate ahm saadhan banataa he
 The increase in repo rate by RBI helps in controlling inflation
 jab bhi arabiai repo rate badhaata he, to bank usase kam karj lete hai
 Due to this, money supply is less in circulation
 isse mahangaai par niyantran paane main madad milti he
 This effect on you is the increase in the repo rate means that the funds that banks will take from RBI, they will get it at expensive rates
 isse bainkon par dabaav badhata he
 To reduce their burden, banks pass it on to customers
 yah boj aapke saath mahange karj or badi hui iemai ke taur par baanta jaataa he
 For this reason, whenever the repo rate increases, it becomes expensive for you to take a loan
 bataa den ki bhartiya rigerv bank ne farvari main bhi byaaj daron main koi badlaav nahin kiya
